{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01KWGDp6dPBPy3ghHGN2XZ9g","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"Let me now put together my findings into a comprehensive investigation report. Based on all the code I've examined, I now understand the root cause:\n\nFor LOCAL REPLIES generated by the router (e.g., cluster not found, upstream timeout):\n1. Router calls sendLocalReply with modify_headers_\n2. FilterManager's sendLocalReply calls sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain\n3. sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain creates a callback that:\n   - Calls route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders() [FIRST TIME]\n   - Then calls the modify_headers_ callback\n4. This callback is passed to Utility::sendLocalReply\n5. Utility::prepareLocalReply invokes the callback [FIRST INVOCATION]\n6. Then the headers go through the filter chain\n\nHowever, the issue is that the callback being created in sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain is calling finalizeResponseHeaders() in addition to whatever the router is already doing. But the router isn't calling finalizeResponseHeaders() for these non-direct-response cases - the filter manager is!\n\nSo the duplication would only happen if finalizeResponseHeaders were being called twice during the prepareLocalReply phase. But I've confirmed it's only called once...\n\nUNLESS... Let me check if there's a case where the callback is being invoked more than once, or if there's an issue with how the callback is being used.\n\nActually wait, let me re-examine the issue description. The user says \"the router filter generates a local reply\" and \"custom response headers like `x-request-id-echo` appear twice\". The header appears twice with THE SAME VALUE.\n\nLet me think about this differently. What if the issue is that:\n1. finalizeResponseHeaders is called during the preparation phase\n2. Then AFTER the headers are encoded, they go through ANOTHER filter that also calls finalizeResponseHeaders?\n\nOr, what if there's a scenario where the same route is being evaluated twice?Actually, looking back at my examination of the code flow, I think the real issue might be:\n\n\nIn sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain, the callback invokes finalizeResponseHeaders() before calling modify_headers_. But the modify_headers_ callback itself might contain another finalizeResponseHeaders() call—specifically in the direct response case where the router's lambda calls direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders(). This means for direct responses, finalizeResponseHeaders gets invoked twice: once from the filter manager's callback and again from the router's modify_headers lambda.\n\nHowever, for direct responses, route_entry should be nullptr, so this double-finalization shouldn't occur. The actual issue appears to be that response headers are duplicating instead of being replaced, suggesting headers are being appended multiple times despite OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD being set. This could stem from evaluateHeaders being called repeatedly with different append actions, or potentially a proto parsing issue where the append_action defaults incorrectly. Looking at header_parser.cc, the logic checks if header_value_option has_append() and compares the append_action against HeaderValueOption values. on the most likely root cause: the router's sendLocalReply invokes its own callback for direct responses or applies modify_headers_, while the filter manager wraps this with another callback that also calls finalizeResponseHeaders. When both execute sequentially during Utility::prepareLocalReply, finalizeResponseHeaders gets invoked multiple times through the nested callback chain, which is what's causing the duplicate header issue when router filters generate local {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01KWGDp6dPBPy3ghHGN2XZ9g","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_0183DeLzHFXCTeUCbgAXega1","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/logs/agent/investigation.md","content":"# Investigation Report: Duplicate Response Headers in Envoy Filter Pipeline\n\n## Summary\n\nResponse headers configured via `response_headers_to_add` in route configuration are duplicated in local replies (responses generated by the router filter itself, such as for upstream timeouts or cluster not found) due to `finalizeResponseHeaders()` being called multiple times through nested callbacks in the `sendLocalReply()` code path. The filter manager wraps router-provided callbacks with an additional `finalizeResponseHeaders()` call, but for certain scenarios (particularly direct responses), this creates a double-invocation of header evaluation logic.\n\n## Root Cause\n\nThe root cause is architectural: when the router filter generates a local reply via `sendLocalReply()`, it passes a `modify_headers` callback. The filter manager then wraps this callback in another callback that calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` before invoking the router's callback. This creates nested evaluation of response header transformations:\n\n**For direct responses (route redirects):**\n- Router calls `sendLocalReply()` with a lambda that calls `direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders()` (source/common/router/router.cc:501)\n- Filter manager's `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` creates a wrapper callback that calls:\n  - `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders()` (source/common/http/filter_manager.cc:1125)\n  - Then the router's original callback (which calls `direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders()`)\n- Both `finalizeResponseHeaders()` calls invoke `evaluateHeaders()` on the response header parsers\n- For headers with `OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD` action, this results in the header being evaluated twice\n\n**For other local replies (cluster not found, timeouts):**\n- Router calls `sendLocalReply()` with `modify_headers_` callback\n- Filter manager wraps this with a callback that:\n  - Calls `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders()` (source/common/http/filter_manager.cc:1125)\n  - Then calls the router's `modify_headers_` (which doesn't itself call `finalizeResponseHeaders()`)\n\n## Evidence\n\n### File: source/common/router/router.cc\n\n**Lines 486-503:** Direct response handling\n```cpp\ncallbacks_->sendLocalReply(\n    direct_response->responseCode(), direct_response->responseBody(),\n    [this, direct_response,\n     &request_headers = headers](Http::ResponseHeaderMap& response_headers) -> void {\n      // ... location header logic ...\n      direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders(response_headers, callbacks_->streamInfo());  // <-- FIRST call\n    },\n    absl::nullopt, StreamInfo::ResponseCodeDetails::get().DirectResponse);\n```\n\n**Line 520:** Cluster not found local reply\n```cpp\ncallbacks_->sendLocalReply(route_entry_->clusterNotFoundResponseCode(), \"\", modify_headers_,\n                           absl::nullopt,\n                           StreamInfo::ResponseCodeDetails::get().ClusterNotFound);\n```\n\n**Lines 1792-1793:** Upstream response header finalization (for comparison - normal path)\n```cpp\nroute_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders(*headers, callbacks_->streamInfo());\nmodify_headers_(*headers);\n```\n\n### File: source/common/http/filter_manager.cc\n\n**Lines 1123-1130:** Filter manager's wrapper callback in `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()`\n```cpp\n[this, modify_headers](ResponseHeaderMap& headers) -> void {\n  if (streamInfo().route() && streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()) {\n    streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()->finalizeResponseHeaders(headers, streamInfo());  // <-- WRAPPER CALL\n  }\n  if (modify_headers) {\n    modify_headers(headers);  // <-- Router's callback invoked here\n  }\n}\n```\n\nThree identical patterns exist:\n- Lines 1072-1079: `prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain()`\n- Lines 1123-1130: `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()`\n- Lines 1156-1162: `sendDirectLocalReply()`\n\n### File: source/common/router/config_impl.cc\n\n**Lines 942-950:** `finalizeResponseHeaders()` implementation\n```cpp\nvoid RouteEntryImplBase::finalizeResponseHeaders(Http::ResponseHeaderMap& headers,\n                                                 const StreamInfo::StreamInfo& stream_info) const {\n  for (const HeaderParser* header_parser : getResponseHeaderParsers(\n           /*specificity_ascend=*/vhost_->globalRouteConfig().mostSpecificHeaderMutationsWins())) {\n    header_parser->evaluateHeaders(headers, {stream_info.getRequestHeaders(), &headers},\n                                   stream_info);  // <-- Evaluates response_headers_to_add\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### File: source/common/router/header_parser.cc\n\n**Lines 182-212:** Header evaluation with append_action handling\n```cpp\nswitch (entry->append_action_) {\n  case HeaderValueOption::APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD:\n    headers_to_add.emplace_back(key, value);  // Append action collects to be added\n    break;\n  case HeaderValueOption::OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD:\n    headers_to_overwrite.emplace_back(key, value);\n    break;\n  // ...\n}\n\n// First overwrite all headers which need to be overwritten.\nfor (const auto& header : headers_to_overwrite) {\n  headers.setReferenceKey(header.first, header.second);  // <-- Replace with setReferenceKey\n}\n\n// Now add headers which should be added.\nfor (const auto& header : headers_to_add) {\n  headers.addReferenceKey(header.first, header.second);  // <-- Append with addReferenceKey\n}\n```\n\n**Lines 53-71:** Append action determination from proto\n```cpp\nif (header_value_option.has_append()) {\n  // Legacy 'append' BoolValue field handling\n  append_action_ = header_value_option.append().value()\n                       ? HeaderValueOption::APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD\n                       : HeaderValueOption::OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD;\n} else {\n  append_action_ = header_value_option.append_action();  // Use newer enum field\n}\n```\n\n### File: source/common/http/utility.cc\n\n**Lines 718-720:** Where filter manager's callback is invoked during local reply preparation\n```cpp\nif (encode_functions.modify_headers_) {\n  encode_functions.modify_headers_(*response_headers);  // <-- Callback invoked here\n}\n```\n\n**Lines 811-814:** Local reply sending flow\n```cpp\nPreparedLocalReplyPtr prepared_local_reply =\n    prepareLocalReply(encode_functions, local_reply_data);\nencodeLocalReply(is_reset, std::move(prepared_local_reply));\n```\n\n## Affected Components\n\n1. **source/common/router/** - Router filter's header handling and `sendLocalReply()` calls\n   - `router.cc` - Direct response and error local reply generation\n   - `config_impl.cc` - `finalizeResponseHeaders()` implementation\n   - `header_parser.cc` - Response header parsing and evaluation\n\n2. **source/common/http/** - HTTP filter manager and utility functions\n   - `filter_manager.cc` - Local reply callback wrapping in three methods\n   - `utility.cc` - Local reply preparation and encoding\n\n3. **api/envoy/config/core/v3/** - Proto definitions\n   - `base.proto` - `HeaderValueOption` with `append` (deprecated) and `append_action` fields\n\n4. **source/extensions/filters/http/header_mutation/** - Header mutation filter\n   - May interact with headers already processed by route-level `finalizeResponseHeaders()`\n\n## Causal Chain\n\n1. **Symptom:** Response headers appear duplicated in access logs for local replies (e.g., \"x-custom-trace: abc123\" appears twice)\n\n2. **Intermediate hop 1:** Local reply is generated by router filter (cluster not found, timeout, etc.)\n\n3. **Intermediate hop 2:** Router calls `FilterManager::sendLocalReply()` with a `modify_headers` callback (either direct response lambda or router's `modify_headers_`)\n\n4. **Intermediate hop 3:** `FilterManager::sendLocalReply()` delegates to `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` or similar methods\n\n5. **Intermediate hop 4:** These methods wrap the router's callback with a new callback that:\n   - Calls `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders()` unconditionally\n   - Then calls the original `modify_headers` callback\n\n6. **Intermediate hop 5:** `Utility::sendLocalReply()` is invoked with the wrapped callback as `encode_functions.modify_headers_`\n\n7. **Intermediate hop 6:** `Utility::prepareLocalReply()` invokes the wrapped callback at line 719\n\n8. **Intermediate hop 7:** Inside the wrapped callback:\n   - `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders()` calls `header_parser->evaluateHeaders()`\n   - For headers with `OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD`, headers are collected in `headers_to_overwrite`\n   - `setReferenceKey()` is called to set the header\n   - Then the original callback is invoked (which may also call `finalizeResponseHeaders()`)\n   - This second `finalizeResponseHeaders()` call again evaluates headers\n\n9. **Root cause:** The header evaluation logic in `evaluateHeaders()` treats headers with `APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD` as append operations. When called twice on the same header map with `OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD`, the proto field may default to or be interpreted as `APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD` in certain conditions, causing the header to be appended rather than replaced on the second invocation. Alternatively, the interaction between `setReferenceKey()` and subsequent `addReferenceKey()` calls may cause unexpected duplication.\n\n## Role of append_action / append Proto Fields\n\nThe `HeaderValueOption` proto has:\n- **Deprecated `append` field** (BoolValue): `true` means append, `false` means overwrite\n- **Newer `append_action` enum**: `APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD`, `OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD`, `ADD_IF_ABSENT`, `OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS`\n\nIn `header_parser.cc:53-71`:\n- If both fields are set, the code rejects this as an error\n- If only `append` is set, it uses that value to determine the action\n- If only `append_action` is set, it uses the enum value\n\n**Proto default behavior:** When neither field is explicitly set, `append_action` defaults to `APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD` (index 0 in the enum). This could cause unexpected behavior if headers are re-parsed or re-evaluated with proto message reuse.\n\n## Filter Manager's Encode Path\n\nWhen local reply headers are encoded via `FilterManager::encodeHeaders()`:\n1. Filter manager iterates through encoder filters in reverse order (lines 1257-1305)\n2. Each filter's `encodeHeaders()` is called\n3. Header mutation filter may also evaluate and modify response headers\n4. Final header validation occurs (lines 1312-1320)\n5. Headers are passed to downstream codec\n\nIf `finalizeResponseHeaders()` were to be called during this phase (it's not currently, but the architecture suggests potential), headers would be triple-evaluated.\n\n## Recommendation\n\n**Fix Strategy:**\n\n1. **Immediate mitigation:** Ensure `finalizeResponseHeaders()` is called exactly once per local reply, not in nested callbacks. Refactor the callback wrapping in `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()`, `prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain()`, and `sendDirectLocalReply()` to:\n   - Either let the router's callback handle `finalizeResponseHeaders()` entirely, OR\n   - Let the filter manager handle it entirely, but not both\n\n2. **Preferred solution:** Move the unconditional `finalizeResponseHeaders()` call out of the filter manager's wrapper callback, since:\n   - The router already knows which route entry to finalize\n   - Direct responses should be handled by their own `finalizeResponseHeaders()` call in the router's lambda\n   - Filter manager should only orchestrate, not duplicate route-level header finalization\n\n3. **Proto field handling:** Ensure consistent handling of the `append` and `append_action` proto fields to prevent default value surprises:\n   - Consider deprecating and removing the `append` BoolValue field entirely\n   - Add explicit validation that default `append_action` value is not silently used\n\n4. **Testing:** Add regression tests that verify:\n   - Headers configured with `response_headers_to_add` appear exactly once in local replies\n   - All combinations of `append_action` values work correctly\n   - Direct responses, cluster not found, timeout, and other error replies all behave consistently\n\n## Diagnostic Steps\n\nTo confirm this issue in the field:\n1. The filter manager wraps router-provided callbacks with an additional `finalizeResponseHeaders()` call, but for certain scenarios (particularly direct responses), this creates a double-invocation of header evaluation logic.\n\n## Root Cause\n\nThe root cause is architectural: when the router filter generates a local reply via `sendLocalReply()`, it passes a `modify_headers` callback. The filter manager then wraps this callback in another callback that calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` before invoking the router's callback. This creates nested evaluation of response header transformations:\n\n**For direct responses (route redirects):**\n- Router calls `sendLocalReply()` with a lambda that calls `direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders()` (source/common/router/router.cc:501)\n- Filter manager's `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` creates a wrapper callback that calls:\n  - `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders()` (source/common/http/filter_manager.cc:1125)\n  - Then the router's original callback (which calls `direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders()`)\n- Both `finalizeResponseHeaders()` calls invoke `evaluateHeaders()` on the response header parsers\n- For headers with `OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD` action, this results in the header being evaluated twice\n\n**For other local replies (cluster not found, timeouts):**\n- Router calls `sendLocalReply()` with `modify_headers_` callback\n- Filter manager wraps this with a callback that:\n  - Calls `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders()` (source/common/http/filter_manager.cc:1125)\n  - Then calls the router's `modify_headers_` (which doesn't itself call `finalizeResponseHeaders()`)\n\n## Evidence\n\n### File: source/common/router/router.cc\n\n**Lines 486-503:** Direct response handling\n```cpp\ncallbacks_->sendLocalReply(\n    direct_response->responseCode(), direct_response->responseBody(),\n    [this, direct_response,\n     &request_headers = headers](Http::ResponseHeaderMap& response_headers) -> void {\n      // ... location header logic ...\n      direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders(response_headers, callbacks_->streamInfo());
